$("#hideButton").hover(
	function() {
		$("#hideButton").addClass("buttonHover");
	},
	function() {
		$("#hideButton").removeClass("buttonHover");	
	}	
);

$("#button1").hover(
	function() {
		$("#button1").addClass("tabHover");
	},
	function() {
		$("#button1").removeClass("tabHover");	
	}	
);
	
$("#button2").hover(
	function() {
		$("#button2").addClass("tabHover");
	},
	function() {
		$("#button2").removeClass("tabHover");	
	}	
);
	
$("#button3").hover(
	function() {
		$("#button3").addClass("tabHover");
	},
	function() {
		$("#button3").removeClass("tabHover");	
	}
);


	$("#hideButton").toggle(

	function() {
		$("#tabPages").slideUp();

		$("#button1").removeClass("active");
		$('.modal-hover').css({ 'display': 'none' });
		$("#button2").removeClass("active");
		$("#button3").removeClass("active");	

		$("#hideImage").attr('src','/sites/all/themes/sglasnik/images/Prodaja_arrow_close.jpg');
			
		
		/*scrollTo(0,999999);*/
	},
	function() {
		$("#page1").show();
		$("#page2").hide();
		$("#page3").hide();	

		$("#button1").addClass("active");
		$("#button2").removeClass("active");
		$("#button3").removeClass("active");
		
		$("#tabPages").slideDown();
		
		$("#hideImage").attr('src','/sites/all/themes/sglasnik/images/Prodaja_arrow_open.jpg');
	}	
	);

	$("#button1").click(function() {
		$("#page1").show();
		$("#page2").hide();
		$("#page3").hide();

       <script type="text/javascript">
        function search() {
									var q = document.getElementById('query').value.trim();
									if(q === '') {
										//window.location = "http://www.pravno-informacioni-sistem.rs/SlGlasnikPortal/fp/unifiedSearch";
										window.open('https://www.pravno-informacioni-sistem.rs/SlGlasnikPortal/fp/unifiedSearch');
									} else {
										// window.location = "http://www.pravno-informacioni-sistem.rs/SlGlasnikPortal/fp/unifiedSearch?q=" + q;
										window.open('https://www.pravno-informacioni-sistem.rs/SlGlasnikPortal/fp/unifiedSearch?q=' + q);
									}
								}
       </script>

       jssor_slider2_starter = function (containerId) {
            var options = {
                $AutoPlay: true,                                    //[Optional] Whether to auto play, to enable slideshow, this option must be set to true, default value is false
                $AutoPlaySteps: 1,                                  //[Optional] Steps to go for each navigation request (this options applys only when slideshow disabled), the default value is 1
                $AutoPlayInterval: 4000,                            //[Optional] Interval (in milliseconds) to go for next slide since the previous stopped if the slider is auto playing, default value is 3000
                $PauseOnHover: 1,                               //[Optional] Whether to pause when mouse over if a slider is auto playing, 0 no pause, 1 pause for desktop, 2 pause for touch device, 3 pause for desktop and touch device, 4 freeze for desktop, 8 freeze for touch device, 12 freeze for desktop and touch device, default value is 1

                $ArrowKeyNavigation: true,   			            //[Optional] Allows keyboard (arrow key) navigation or not, default value is false
                $SlideDuration: 500,                                //[Optional] Specifies default duration (swipe) for slide in milliseconds, default value is 500
                $MinDragOffsetToSlide: 20,                          //[Optional] Minimum drag offset to trigger slide , default value is 20
                //$SlideWidth: 960,                                 //[Optional] Width of every slide in pixels, default value is width of 'slides' container
                //$SlideHeight: 280,                                //[Optional] Height of every slide in pixels, default value is height of 'slides' container
                $SlideSpacing: 0, 					                //[Optional] Space between each slide in pixels, default value is 0
                $DisplayPieces: 1,                                  //[Optional] Number of pieces to display (the slideshow would be disabled if the value is set to greater than 1), the default value is 1
                $ParkingPosition: 0,                                //[Optional] The offset position to park slide (this options applys only when slideshow disabled), default value is 0.
                $UISearchMode: 1,                                   //[Optional] The way (0 parellel, 1 recursive, default value is 1) to search UI components (slides container, loading screen, navigator container, arrow navigator container, thumbnail navigator container etc).
                $PlayOrientation: 1,                                //[Optional] Orientation to play slide (for auto play, navigation), 1 horizental, 2 vertical, 5 horizental reverse, 6 vertical reverse, default value is 1
                $DragOrientation: 3,                                //[Optional] Orientation to drag slide, 0 no drag, 1 horizental, 2 vertical, 3 either, default value is 1 (Note that the $DragOrientation should be the same as $PlayOrientation when $DisplayPieces is greater than 1, or parking position is not 0)

                $ArrowNavigatorOptions: {
                    $Class: $JssorArrowNavigator$,              //[Requried] Class to create arrow navigator instance
                    $ChanceToShow: 1,                               //[Required] 0 Never, 1 Mouse Over, 2 Always
                    $AutoCenter: 2,                                 //[Optional] Auto center arrows in parent container, 0 No, 1 Horizontal, 2 Vertical, 3 Both, default value is 0
                    $Steps: 1                                       //[Optional] Steps to go for each navigation request, default value is 1
                },

                $ThumbnailNavigatorOptions: {
                    $Class: $JssorThumbnailNavigator$,              //[Required] Class to create thumbnail navigator instance
                    $ChanceToShow: 2,                               //[Required] 0 Never, 1 Mouse Over, 2 Always

                    $ActionMode: 1,                                 //[Optional] 0 None, 1 act by click, 2 act by mouse hover, 3 both, default value is 1
                    $AutoCenter: 3,                                 //[Optional] Auto center thumbnail items in the thumbnail navigator container, 0 None, 1 Horizontal, 2 Vertical, 3 Both, default value is 3
                    $Lanes: 1,                                      //[Optional] Specify lanes to arrange thumbnails, default value is 1
                    $SpacingX: 3,                                   //[Optional] Horizontal space between each thumbnail in pixel, default value is 0
                    $SpacingY: 3,                                   //[Optional] Vertical space between each thumbnail in pixel, default value is 0
                    $DisplayPieces: 9,                              //[Optional] Number of pieces to display, default value is 1
                    $ParkingPosition: 260,                          //[Optional] The offset position to park thumbnail
                    $Orientation: 1,                                //[Optional] Orientation to arrange thumbnails, 1 horizental, 2 vertical, default value is 1
                    $DisableDrag: false                            //[Optional] Disable drag or not, default value is false
                }
            };

            var jssor_slider2 = new $JssorSlider$(containerId, options);
            //responsive code begin
            //you can remove responsive code if you don't want the slider scales while window resizes
            function ScaleSlider() {
                var parentWidth = jssor_slider2.$Elmt.parentNode.clientWidth;
                if (parentWidth)
                    jssor_slider2.$ScaleWidth(Math.min(parentWidth, 960));
                else
                    $Jssor$.$Delay(ScaleSlider, 30);
            }

            ScaleSlider();
            $Jssor$.$AddEvent(window, "load", ScaleSlider);

            $Jssor$.$AddEvent(window, "resize", $Jssor$.$WindowResizeFilter(window, ScaleSlider));
            $Jssor$.$AddEvent(window, "orientationchange", ScaleSlider);
            //responsive code end
        };
      </script>
      <!-- Jssor Slider Begin -->

           25. Мај 2018.
          </div>
          <div class="title2">
           <a href="/%D0%B0%D0%BA%D1%82%D1%83%D0%B5%D0%BB%D0%BD%D0%BE/%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B8/%D0%B3%D0%BB%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BA-%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B4%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B8%D0%BE-%D0%BC%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B0%D1%84%D0%B8%D1%98%D1%83-%D0%BE-%D0%B1%D0%B5%D0%BE%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B4%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BC-%D1%84%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B8%D0%B2%D0%B0%D0%BB%D1%83-%D0%B8%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B5">
            Гласник представио монографију о Београдском фестивалу игре
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="intro">
           <p style="text-align: justify;">
            У Клубу – књижари – галерији
            <i>
             Гласник
            </i>
            , у петак
            <a href="/%D0%B0%D0%BA%D1%82%D1%83%D0%B5%D0%BB%D0%BD%D0%BE/%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B8/%D0%B3%D0%BB%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BA-%D0%BF%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B4%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B8%D0%BE-%D0%BC%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B0%D1%84%D0%B8%D1%98%D1%83-%D0%BE-%D0%B1%D0%B5%D0%BE%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%B4%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BC-%D1%84%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B8%D0%B2%D0%B0%D0%BB%D1%83-%D0%B8%D0%B3%D1%80%D0%B5">

        <div id="sectionHeader">
         Изузев каталога за 2014, 2015, 2016. и 2017. годину, цене у каталозима за претходне године не обухватају промену пореске стопе предвиђену
         <br/>
         Законом о изменама Закона о порезу на додату вредност који се примењује од 1. јануара 2014.

      <!-- modal_panels -->
      <div class="modal modal-hover" id="modal_hover_span_1">
       <span class="arrow-up">
       </span>
       <div class="modal-content">
        <div class="images">
        </div>
        <div class="map">
        </div>
       </div>
       <span class="arrow-down">
       </span>
      </div>
      <div class="modal modal-img" id="modal_img">
       <div class="modal-content">
        <span class="close" id="close">
         ✖
        </span>
        <img alt="" src=""/>
        <span class="info">
        </span>
       </div>
      </div>
      <!-- modal_panels kraj -->
      <!-- додајем нови ред, како бих проверио да ли свима долази емаЈл са информацијом о измени у фајлу -->
      <script type="text/javascript">
       var timer = null;
        var position_top = 0;

        function on_close_img() {
            jQuery('#modal_img').css({ 'display': 'none' });
            start_timer();
            jQuery('body').css({'overflow':'auto'});
            window.scrollTo(0, position_top);
        }

        function start_timer() {
            if (timer !== null) {
                clearTimeout(timer);
            }
            timer = setTimeout(function () {
                jQuery('.modal-hover').css({ 'display': 'none' });
                timer = null;
            }, 1500);   // 1500 ms
        }

        // zatvaranje modal_hover-a sa kašnjenjem
        function on_leave() {
            var modal_img = document.getElementById('modal_img');
            // ne treba zatvarati ako je otvorena slika
            if (modal_img.style.display != "block") {
                start_timer();
            }
        }

        function is_ie() {
            if(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf("msie") > -1 || navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf("11.") > -1) {
                return true;
            }
            else {
                return false;
            }
        }

        jQuery('#close').click(on_close_img);

        window.onclick = function(event) {
            if (jQuery(event.target).attr('id') == 'modal_img') {
                on_close_img();
            }
        };

        jQuery(".location-images").hover(function(enter) {
            // zatvori svaki modalni panel na početku i resetuje id
            jQuery('.modal-hover').css({ 'display': 'none' }).attr('id','modal_hover_span');

            // informacija o lokaciji knjižare
            var info = jQuery(this).next('.location-info').text() + ", " + jQuery(this).siblings('.location-town').text();

            // id elementa na hover sa klasom .location-images
            var init = jQuery(this).attr('id');
            var gallery = init.substr(5);
            jQuery('#modal_hover_span').attr('id','modal_hover_' + init);

            // menja modalni panel u zavisnosti od vrednosti promenljive init
            var modal_hover = document.getElementById('modal_hover_' + init);

            // prolazi kroz slike i formira link do njih
            var img_tag = '';
            var map = '';
            for(var i = 1; i<5; i++) {
                var src = '/sites/all/themes/sglasnik/images/knjizare/' +gallery+ '/' +i+ '.jpg';
                var map_src = '/sites/all/themes/sglasnik/images/knjizare/' +gallery+ '/map.jpg';
                img_tag += '<a href="#"><img alt="" src="'+src+'" /></a>';
                map = '<a href="#"><img alt="" src="'+map_src+'" /></a>';
            }
            jQuery('#modal_hover_' + init + ' .modal-content .images').html(img_tag);
            jQuery('#modal_hover_' + init + ' .modal-content .map').html(map);

            // enter.target je element sa klasom .location-images
            modal_hover.style.display = "block";

            // pozicija elementa sa klasom .location
            var bbox = enter.target.getBoundingClientRect();

            if(is_ie()) {
                jQuery("#" + modal_hover.getAttribute('id')).css({
                    'top': bbox.top + document.documentElement.scrollTop + 24 + "px",
                    'left': bbox.left + 4 + "px"
                });
                position_top = bbox.top + document.documentElement.scrollTop + 24;
            }
            else {
                jQuery("#" + modal_hover.getAttribute('id')).css({
                    'top': bbox.top + window.scrollY + 24 + "px",
                    'left': bbox.left + 4 + "px"
                });
                position_top = bbox.top + window.scrollY + 24;
            }

            var scroll_top = (window.pageYOffset !== undefined) ? window.pageYOffset : (document.documentElement || document.body.parentNode || document.body).scrollTop;

            if((position_top-scroll_top) > 500) {
                jQuery("#" + modal_hover.getAttribute('id')).css({
                    'top': position_top - 380 + "px",
                    'left': bbox.left + 4 + "px"
                });
                jQuery('.arrow-up').css({'display':'none'});
                jQuery('.arrow-down').css({'display':'block'});
                jQuery('.modal-content').css({'box-shadow':'10px -10px 5px #cccccc', 'margin':'1% 1% 0'});
            }
            else {
                jQuery('.arrow-up').css({'display':'block'});
                jQuery('.arrow-down').css({'display':'none'});
                jQuery('.modal-content').css({'box-shadow':'10px 10px 5px #cccccc', 'margin':'0 1% 1%'});
            }

			// klik na sliku pokreće novi modalni panel sa tom slikom
            jQuery("#" + modal_hover.getAttribute('id') + " a img").click(function() {
                var modal_img = document.getElementById('modal_img');
                var modal_img_src = jQuery(this).attr('src');
                var len = modal_img_src.length;
                console.log(jQuery(this).attr('src'));
                // poziva veliku sliku za pojedinačni prikaz
                jQuery("#modal_img img").attr('src', modal_img_src.substr(0,len-4)+'-large.jpg');
                console.log(modal_img_src.substr(0,len-4)+'-large.jpg');
                jQuery("#modal_img .info").text(info);
                modal_img.style.display = "block";
                jQuery('body').css({'overflow':'hidden'});
            });
        }, on_leave);

        jQuery('.modal-hover').hover(function() {
            if(timer !== null) {
                clearTimeout(timer);
            }
        }, on_leave);
      </script>
     </div>
